Section 1:
1 ENGR OSSED HOUSE
JOINT
2 RESOLUTION NO. 1069 By: Lawson of the House
3 and
4 Thompson of the Senate
5
6
to refer to the people for their approval or
8 rejection proposed amendments to Sections 4 and 8 of
Article XVII of the Constitution of the State of
9 Oklahoma; modifying procedure for the Legislature to
create or alter counties and the equitable division
10 of assets and liabilities; providing updated legal
descriptions of counties; providing ballot title; and
11 directing filing.
12
13
14 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE HOUSE OF REPRESENTATIVES AND THE SENATE
15 OF THE 2ND SESSION OF THE 60TH OKLAHOMA LEGISLATURE:
16 SECTION 1. The Secretary of State shall refer to the people for
17 their approval or rejection, as and in the manner provided by law,
18 the following proposed amendment to Section 4 of Article XVII of the
19 Constitution of the State of Oklahoma to read as follows:
20 Section 4. The Legislature shall provide by general laws for
21 the creation of new counties or altering or changing lines and the
22 equitable division of assets and of liabilities, and the original
23 location of county seats in such new counties: Provided, That every
24 such question shall be submitted to the vote of the qualified
ENGR. H. J. R. NO. 1069 Page 1
1 elec tors residing in the territory to be formed into such new county
2 or transferred to another county, and shall be approved by sixty per
3 centum of the votes cast in said election: Provided, That no new
4 county shall be formed of less than four hundred square miles
5 taxable area, nor with a population less than fifteen thousand
6 people, nor with taxable wealth less than two and one-half million
7 dollars, as shown by the current tax rolls. Nor shall any territory
8 be taken from an existing county for any purpose bringing the newly
9 created line of such existing county nearer than ten miles to the
10 county seat thereof. Nor shall the taxable area, population, or
11 taxable wealth of said existing county be reduced below that
12 required for a new county. Nor shall any territory, in any case, be
13 transferred from one county to an existing county, if, by such
14 transfer of territory, the county from which the territory be taken
15 will then be smaller in area than the county to which the addition
16 is made: Provided, That when territory is to be transferred from an
17 existing county to either a new or an existing county, there must be
18 sixty per centum of the vote cast in such particular territory in
19 favor of the transfer, and, in case the transfer be to an existing
20 county, the acceptance of such territory must first be approved by a
21 majority vote of the electors of said county, at an election to be
22 called and held therefor, as may be provided by law. The limitation
23 as to area, valuation and population shall not be increased by the
24 Legislature.
ENGR. H. J. R. NO. 1069 Page 2
1 SECTION 2. The Secretary of State shall refer to the people for
2 their approval or rejection, as and in the manner provided by law,
3 the following proposed amendment to Section 8 of Article XVII of the
4 Constitution of the State of Oklahoma to read as follows:
5 Section 8. The State of Oklahoma is hereby divided into
6 Counties named and described as follows (all descriptions are
7 referred to the Indian Meridian and base line established by the
8 United States Geological Survey, 1895-1899; unless otherwise
9 specifically mentioned). Detailed Public Land Survey System (PLSS)
10 descriptions are referenced to the Bureau of Land Management (BLM)
11 New Mexico CADNSDI PLSS Township, First Division (Sections) and
12 Second Division (Section subdivisions and government lots)
13 Geographic Information System (GIS) vector digital data layers,
14 Version 2, published December 13, 2023:
15 Adair County: Beginning on the township line between townships
16 nineteen and twenty North, at its intersection with the range line
17 between ranges twenty-three and twenty-four East; thence east along
18 said township line to its intersection with the Arkansas State line;
19 thence southward along said Arkansas State line to its intersection
20 with the township line between townships thirteen and fourteen
21 North; thence west along said township line to its intersection with
22 the range line between ranges twenty-three and twenty-four East;
23 thence north along said range line to the point of beginning.
24 Westville is hereby designated the County Seat of Adair County.

ENGR. H. J. R. NO. 1069 Page 150
1 SECTION 3. The Ballot Title for the proposed Constitutional
2 amendment as set forth in SECTIONS 1 and 2 of this resolution shall
3 be in the following form:
4 BALLOT TITLE
5 Legislative Referendum No. ____ State Question No. ____
6 THE GIST OF THE PROPOSITION IS AS FOLLOWS:
7 This measure amends the Oklahoma Constitution in Sections 4 and
8 8 of Article 17. This measure updates the provisions related
9 to the creation of new counties and changes to county
10 boundaries. This measure would still allow the Legislature to
11 pass general laws governing the creation of new counties,
12 changes to county lines, the fair division of county assets and
13 debts, and the original location of county seats. All other
14 requirements including voting requirements to form a county or
15 transfer territory and minimum requirements for land area,
16 population size, and taxable property value which are currently
17 listed in the Constitution would be stricken. These
18 requirements would still be governed by statutes passed by the
19 Legislature. This measure also provides updated legal
20 descriptions of all seventy-seven counties.
21 SHALL THE PROPOSAL BE APPROVED?
22 FOR THE PROPOSAL — YES _____________
23 AGAINST THE PROPOSAL — NO _____________
24
ENGR. H. J. R. NO. 1069 Page 151

2 immediately after the passage of this resolution, shall prepare and
3 file one copy thereof, including the Ballot Title set forth in
4 SECTION 3 hereof, with the Secretary of State and one copy with the
5 Attorney General.
6 Passed the House of Representatives the 25th day of March, 2026.

1 ENGR OSSED HOUSE
JOINT
2 RESOLUTION NO. 1069 By: Lawson of the House
3 and
4 Thompson of the Senate
5
6
7 A Joint Resolution directing the Secretary of State
to refer to the people for their approval or
8 rejection proposed amendments to Sections 4 and 8 of
Article XVII of the Constitution of the State of
9 Oklahoma; modifying procedure for the Legislature to
create or alter counties and the equitable division
10 of assets and liabilities; providing updated legal
descriptions of counties; providing ballot title; and
11 directing filing.
12
13
14 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE HOUSE OF REPRESENTATIVES AND THE SENATE
15 OF THE 2ND SESSION OF THE 60TH OKLAHOMA LEGISLATURE:
16 SECTION 1. The Secretary of State shall refer to the people for
17 their approval or rejection, as and in the manner provided by law,
18 the following proposed amendment to Section 4 of Article XVII of the
19 Constitution of the State of Oklahoma to read as follows:
20 Section 4. The Legislature shall provide by general laws for
21 the creation of new counties or altering or changing lines and the
22 equitable division of assets and of liabilities, and the original
23 location of county seats in such new counties: Provided, That every
24 such question shall be submitted to the vote of the qualified
ENGR. H. J. R. NO. 1069 Page 1

1 elec tors residing in the territory to be formed into such new county
2 or transferred to another county, and shall be approved by sixty per
3 centum of the votes cast in said election: Provided, That no new
4 county shall be formed of less than four hundred square miles
5 taxable area, nor with a population less than fifteen thousand
6 people, nor with taxable wealth less than two and one-half million
7 dollars, as shown by the current tax rolls. Nor shall any territory
8 be taken from an existing county for any purpose bringing the newly
9 created line of such existing county nearer than ten miles to the
10 county seat thereof. Nor shall the taxable area, population, or
11 taxable wealth of said existing county be reduced below that
12 required for a new county. Nor shall any territory, in any case, be
13 transferred from one county to an existing county, if, by such
14 transfer of territory, the county from which the territory be taken
15 will then be smaller in area than the county to which the addition
16 is made: Provided, That when territory is to be transferred from an
17 existing county to either a new or an existing county, there must be
18 sixty per centum of the vote cast in such particular territory in
19 favor of the transfer, and, in case the transfer be to an existing
20 county, the acceptance of such territory must first be approved by a
21 majority vote of the electors of said county, at an election to be
22 called and held therefor, as may be provided by law. The limitation
23 as to area, valuation and population shall not be increased by the
24 Legislature.
ENGR. H. J. R. NO. 1069 Page 2

1 SECTION 2. The Secretary of State shall refer to the people for
2 their approval or rejection, as and in the manner provided by law,
3 the following proposed amendment to Section 8 of Article XVII of the
4 Constitution of the State of Oklahoma to read as follows:
5 Section 8. The State of Oklahoma is hereby divided into
6 Counties named and described as follows (all descriptions are
7 referred to the Indian Meridian and base line established by the
8 United States Geological Survey, 1895-1899; unless otherwise
9 specifically mentioned). Detailed Public Land Survey System (PLSS)
10 descriptions are referenced to the Bureau of Land Management (BLM)
11 New Mexico CADNSDI PLSS Township, First Division (Sections) and
12 Second Division (Section subdivisions and government lots)
13 Geographic Information System (GIS) vector digital data layers,
14 Version 2, published December 13, 2023:

21 North; thence west along said township line to its intersection with
22 the range line between ranges twenty-three and twenty-four East;
23 thence north along said range line to the point of beginning.
24 Westville is hereby designated the County Seat of Adair County.

1 SECTION 3. The Ballot Title for the proposed Constitutional
2 amendment as set forth in SECTIONS 1 and 2 of this resolution shall
3 be in the following form:
4 BALLOT TITLE
5 Legislative Referendum No. ____ State Question No. ____
6 THE GIST OF THE PROPOSITION IS AS FOLLOWS:
7 This measure amends the Oklahoma Constitution in Sections 4 and
8 8 of Article 17. This measure updates the provisions related
9 to the creation of new counties and changes to county
10 boundaries. This measure would still allow the Legislature to
11 pass general laws governing the creation of new counties,
12 changes to county lines, the fair division of county assets and
13 debts, and the original location of county seats. All other
14 requirements including voting requirements to form a county or
15 transfer territory and minimum requirements for land area,
16 population size, and taxable property value which are currently
17 listed in the Constitution would be stricken. These
18 requirements would still be governed by statutes passed by the
19 Legislature. This measure also provides updated legal
20 descriptions of all seventy-seven counties.
21 SHALL THE PROPOSAL BE APPROVED?
22 FOR THE PROPOSAL — YES _____________
23 AGAINST THE PROPOSAL — NO _____________

4 SECTION 3 hereof, with the Secretary of State and one copy with the
5 Attorney General.
